### [228] ["The System Will Choose Security Over Humanity Every Time": Understanding Security and Privacy for U.S. Incarcerated Users](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01370)
*Yael Eiger,Nino Migineishvili,Emi Yoshikawa,Liza Nadtochiy,Kentrell Owens,Franziska Roesner*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 美国监狱中数字设备（平板、媒体播放器、信息亭）的使用带来教育、沟通等好处，但也引入隐私安全风险，囚犯缺乏使用自主权且不受消费者保护。研究通过访谈系统受影响人群发现普遍存在的监控、审查、可用性问题，建议平衡监狱安全与隐私需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 监狱中数字设备日益普及，虽然能提供教育、沟通等有益功能，但囚犯在使用这些技术时缺乏自主权，且不受消费者保护法规覆盖，存在严重的隐私和安全风险。需要研究这些技术对系统受影响人群的实际影响。

Method: 通过焦点小组和访谈方式，对17名系统受影响人群（包括前囚犯及其亲属）进行调查，研究他们在使用监狱数字设备时遇到的隐私安全漏洞和权力动态。

Result: 参与者描述了监狱技术中普遍存在的监控、审查和可用性问题，包括不断变化且看似武断的使用政策。这些政策不仅影响囚犯内部关系，也影响与外界的关系，并对囚犯产生负面连锁效应。

Conclusion: 建议通过促进技术相关决策的问责制、提供数字采购和使用政策的公共监督，以及将实际最终用户（囚犯）纳入设计考虑，来更好地平衡监狱安全需求与系统受影响个体的隐私需求。

Abstract: Digital devices like tablets, media players, and kiosks are increasingly deployed in U.S. prisons. These technologies can enable incarcerated people to access education, communicate with loved ones, and develop vital reentry skills. However, they can also introduce new privacy and security risks for incarcerated people who have little agency over their usage and contracts, and are currently carved out of many consumer protection safeguards. To investigate these issues, we conducted focus groups and interviews with system-impacted people (n=17), i.e., those formerly incarcerated, and their relatives, to investigate experiences with device-related security and privacy vulnerabilities and the power dynamics that affect their use. In our findings, participants describe pervasive surveillance, censorship, and usability problems with the technology available to them, including shifting and seemingly arbitrary usage policies. These policies strain relationships both inside and outside prisons and contribute to negative downstream effects for incarcerated users. We recommend ways to better balance prison security concerns with privacy-related needs of system-impacted individuals by promoting accountability for technology-related decisions, providing public oversight of digital purchasing and use policies, and designing digital tools with them -- the actual end-users -- in mind.

</details>


### [229] [Cooking Up Risks: Benchmarking and Reducing Food Safety Risks in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01444)
*Weidi Luo,Xiaofei Wen,Tenghao Huang,Hongyi Wang,Zhen Xiang,Chaowei Xiao,Kristina Gligorić,Muhao Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: FoodGuardBench是首个基于FDA指南的食品安​​全基准测试，包含3339个查询，用于评估LLM在食品相关领域的安全性和鲁棒性，揭示了当前LLM在食品安全领域存在的严重漏洞，并提出了专门的防护模型FoodGuard-4B。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM越来越多地应用于日常任务，包括食品制备和健康指导，但食品安全是一个高风险领域，错误信息可能导致严重的现实危害。当前LLM和安全防护措施缺乏针对特定领域食品危害的严格对齐。

Method: 构建了基于FDA指南的FoodGuardBench基准测试，包含3339个查询，建立了食品安全原则分类体系，并采用代表性越狱攻击（如AutoDAN和PAP）系统评估现有LLM和防护措施。

Result: 评估揭示了三个关键漏洞：1）当前LLM在食品相关领域的安全对齐稀疏，容易受到少数典型越狱策略攻击；2）被攻破时，LLM经常生成可操作但有害的指令，为恶意行为者提供便利；3）现有基于LLM的防护措施系统性地忽视了这些领域特定威胁。

Conclusion: 为缓解这些漏洞，提出了FoodGuard-4B，这是一个在数据集上微调的专业防护模型，用于保护食品相关领域的LLM，填补了领域特定安全对齐的空白。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed for everyday tasks, including food preparation and health-related guidance. However, food safety remains a high-stakes domain where inaccurate or misleading information can cause severe real-world harm. Despite these risks, current LLMs and safety guardrails lack rigorous alignment tailored to domain-specific food hazards. To address this gap, we introduce FoodGuardBench, the first comprehensive benchmark comprising 3,339 queries grounded in FDA guidelines, designed to evaluate the safety and robustness of LLMs. By constructing a taxonomy of food safety principles and employing representative jailbreak attacks (e.g., AutoDAN and PAP), we systematically evaluate existing LLMs and guardrails. Our evaluation results reveal three critical vulnerabilities: First, current LLMs exhibit sparse safety alignment in the food-related domain, easily succumbing to a few canonical jailbreak strategies. Second, when compromised, LLMs frequently generate actionable yet harmful instructions, inadvertently empowering malicious actors and posing tangible risks. Third, existing LLM-based guardrails systematically overlook these domain-specific threats, failing to detect a substantial volume of malicious inputs. To mitigate these vulnerabilities, we introduce FoodGuard-4B, a specialized guardrail model fine-tuned on our datasets to safeguard LLMs within food-related domains.

### [230] [Preserving Target Distributions With Differentially Private Count Mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01468)
*Nitin Kohli,Paul Laskowski*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个两阶段差分隐私框架，用于发布计数表，平衡分布准确性、计数准确性和运行时三个标准。第一阶段使用新的循环拉普拉斯机制估计真实计数分布；第二阶段通过构造算法生成以隐私化分布为不动点的转移矩阵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统差分隐私机制在发布计数表时，虽然保护了个体隐私，但会导致统计偏差。计数分布作为摘要信息，在回答一类研究问题时很有用，但标准隐私化机制会引入统计偏差，这促使研究者提出了"分布准确性"这一新的设计标准。

Method: 研究提出了一个两阶段框架：第一阶段使用专门为计数分布设计的循环拉普拉斯机制来隐私化估计真实计数分布；第二阶段通过构造算法生成转移矩阵，该矩阵的不动点就是隐私化的计数分布。研究者还发展了关于epsilon尺度的数学理论，用于更高效地生成具有良好性质的转移矩阵。

Result: 循环拉普拉斯机制在计数分布隐私化方面优于现有的通用差分隐私直方图机制。新的构造算法比标准优化算法更高效地生成具有良好性质的转移矩阵。实验表明，在特定情况下，不动点方法在性能标准之间提供了有利的权衡。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的两阶段框架和循环拉普拉斯机制为计数表的差分隐私发布提供了更优的解决方案，特别是在需要平衡分布准确性、计数准确性和运行时的情况下。不动点方法在特定应用场景中显示出优越的性能权衡。

Abstract: Differentially private mechanisms are increasingly used to publish tables of counts, where each entry represents the number of individuals belonging to a particular category. A distribution of counts summarizes the information in the count column, unlinking counts from categories. This object is useful for answering a class of research questions, but it is subject to statistical biases when counts are privatized with standard mechanisms. This motivates a novel design criterion we term accuracy of distribution.
  This study formalizes a two-stage framework for privatizing tables of counts that balances accuracy of distribution with two standard criteria of accuracy of counts and runtime. In the first stage, a distribution privatizer generates an estimate for the true distribution of counts. We introduce a new mechanism, called the cyclic Laplace, specifically tailored to distributions of counts, that outperforms existing general-purpose differentially private histogram mechanisms. In the second stage, a constructor algorithm generates a count mechanism, represented as a transition matrix, whose fixed-point is the privatized distribution of counts. We develop a mathematical theory that describes such transition matrices in terms of simple building blocks we call epsilon-scales. This theory informs the design of a new constructor algorithm that generates transition matrices with favorable properties more efficiently than standard optimization algorithms. We explore the practicality of our framework with a set of experiments, highlighting situations in which a fixed-point method provides a favorable tradeoff among performance criteria.

</details>


### [231] [SelfGrader: Stable Jailbreak Detection for Large Language Models using Token-Level Logits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01473)
*Zikai Zhang,Rui Hu,Olivera Kotevska,Jiahao Xu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: SelfGrader是一个轻量级的护栏方法，将越狱检测转化为基于token级logits的数值评分问题，使用数字token的logit分布作为内部安全信号，通过双视角评分规则实现高效检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM护栏方法依赖内部特征或文本响应检测恶意查询，要么引入显著延迟，要么受文本生成随机性影响。需要克服这些限制，开发更高效可靠的越狱检测方法。

Method: 将越狱检测转化为数值评分问题，使用数字token（0-9）的logit分布作为内部安全信号。引入双视角评分规则，同时考虑查询的恶意性和良性，生成稳定可解释的分数。

Result: 在多种越狱基准测试、多个LLM和最先进护栏基线实验中，SelfGrader在LLaMA-3-8B上实现了高达22.66%的ASR降低，同时保持显著更低的内存开销（高达173倍）和延迟（高达26倍）。

Conclusion: SelfGrader通过基于token级logits的数值评分方法，提供了一种高效、轻量级且可靠的LLM越狱检测解决方案，在安全性和效率之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are powerful tools for answering user queries, yet they remain highly vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing guardrail methods typically rely on internal features or textual responses to detect malicious queries, which either introduce substantial latency or suffer from the randomness in text generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose SelfGrader, a lightweight guardrail method that formulates jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using token-level logits. Specifically, SelfGrader evaluates the safety of a user query within a compact set of numerical tokens (NTs) (e.g., 0-9) and interprets their logit distribution as an internal safety signal. To align these signals with human intuition of maliciousness, SelfGrader introduces a dual-perspective scoring rule that considers both the maliciousness and benignness of the query, yielding a stable and interpretable score that reflects harmfulness and reduces the false positive rate simultaneously. Extensive experiments across diverse jailbreak benchmarks, multiple LLMs, and state-of-the-art guardrail baselines demonstrate that SelfGrader achieves up to a 22.66% reduction in ASR on LLaMA-3-8B, while maintaining significantly lower memory overhead (up to 173x) and latency (up to 26x).

</details>

*Yiming Fan,Jun Yeon Won,Ding Zhu,Melih Sirlanci,Mahdi Khalili,Carter Yagemann*

Main category: cs.CR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入EXHIB基准测试，包含从真实世界收集的5个数据集，每个数据集突出BFSD问题空间的不同方面。评估了涵盖多个BFSD范式的9个代表性模型。

Result: 在固件和语义数据集上观察到高达30%的性能下降，揭示了显著的泛化差距。结果表明，对低层和中层二进制变异的鲁棒性无法泛化到高层语义差异。

Conclusion: 当前BFSD评估实践存在关键盲点，需要更全面的基准测试来评估模型在真实世界场景中的泛化能力，特别是在处理固件和语义差异方面。

Abstract: Binary Function Similarity Detection (BFSD) is a core problem in software security, supporting tasks such as vulnerability analysis, malware classification, and patch provenance. In the past few decades, numerous models and tools have been developed for this application; however, due to the lack of a comprehensive universal benchmark in this field, researchers have struggled to compare different models effectively. Existing datasets are limited in scope, often focusing on a narrow set of transformations or types of binaries, and fail to reflect the full diversity of real-world applications.
  We introduce EXHIB, a benchmark comprising five realistic datasets collected from the wild, each highlighting a distinct aspect of the BFSD problem space. We evaluate 9 representative models spanning multiple BFSD paradigms on EXHIB and observe performance degradations of up to 30% on firmware and semantic datasets compared to standard settings, revealing substantial generalization gaps. Our results show that robustness to low- and mid-level binary variations does not generalize to high-level semantic differences, underscoring a critical blind spot in current BFSD evaluation practices.

Abstract: As hardware systems grow in complexity, security verification must keep up with them. This survey synthesizes recent advances in AI-assisted hardware security verification and organizes the literature along key stages of the workflow: asset identification, threat modeling, security test-plan generation, simulation-driven analysis, formal verification, and countermeasure reasoning. To illustrate how these techniques can be applied in practice, we present a case study using the open-source NVIDIA Deep Learning Accelerator (NVDLA), a representative modern hardware design. Throughout this study, we emphasize that while AI/LLM-based automation can significantly accelerate verification tasks, its outputs must remain grounded in simulation evidence, formal reasoning, and benchmark-driven evaluation to ensure trustworthy hardware security assurance.

Method: 集成RTL设计分析、CWE映射和威胁模型智能，利用大语言模型配合自反思精炼机制，确保语法正确性和语义一致性，自动生成安全属性和SystemVerilog断言。

Abstract: The increasing complexity of modern system-on-chip designs amplifies hardware security risks and makes manual security property specification a major bottleneck in formal property verification. Assertain leverages large language models with a self-reflection refinement mechanism to ensure both syntactic correctness and semantic consistency. Evaluated on 11 representative hardware designs, Assertain outperforms GPT-5 by 61.22%, 59.49%, and 67.92% in correct assertion generation, unique CWE coverage, and architectural flaw detection, respectively. These results demonstrate that Assertain significantly expands vulnerability coverage, improves assertion quality, and reduces manual effort in hardware security verification.

### [235] [Diffusion-Guided Adversarial Perturbation Injection for Generalizable Defense Against Facial Manipulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01635)
*Yue Li,Linying Xue,Kaiqing Lin,Hanyu Quan,Dongdong Lin,Hui Tian,Hongxia Wang,Bin Wang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: AEGIS是一种基于扩散模型的对抗性人脸图像生成方法，用于身份保护，通过在DDIM去噪轨迹的潜在空间中注入对抗扰动，突破了传统像素级约束的限制，实现了对GAN和扩散模型深度伪造的有效防御。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GAN和扩散模型的进步使得人脸深度伪造更加真实可控，引发了隐私、安全和身份滥用的严重担忧。现有主动防御方法因次优的扰动注入策略和白盒假设限制，在实际场景中效果有限。

Method: AEGIS提出扩散引导范式，在DDIM去噪轨迹的潜在空间中注入对抗扰动，而非直接修改像素。这种方法解耦了扰动幅度与像素级约束，允许扰动在最有效处自适应放大。同时通过梯度估计策略扩展到黑盒场景。

Result: 在GAN和扩散模型深度伪造生成器上的广泛实验表明，AEGIS在保持高感知质量的同时，始终提供强大的防御效果。在白盒设置中实现稳健的操作破坏，在黑盒设置中展示强大的跨模型可转移性。

Conclusion: AEGIS是首个扩散引导的对抗性人脸图像生成范式，通过潜在空间扰动注入突破了传统防御方法的限制，为实际场景中的深度伪造防御提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in GAN and diffusion models have significantly improved the realism and controllability of facial deepfake manipulation, raising serious concerns regarding privacy, security, and identity misuse. Proactive defenses attempt to counter this threat by injecting adversarial perturbations into images before manipulation takes place. However, existing approaches remain limited in effectiveness due to suboptimal perturbation injection strategies and are typically designed under white-box assumptions, targeting only simple GAN-based attribute editing. These constraints hinder their applicability in practical real-world scenarios. In this paper, we propose AEGIS, the first diffusion-guided paradigm in which the AdvErsarial facial images are Generated for Identity Shielding. We observe that the limited defense capability of existing approaches stems from the peak-clipping constraint, where perturbations are forcibly truncated due to a fixed $L_\infty$-bounded. To overcome this limitation, instead of directly modifying pixels, AEGIS injects adversarial perturbations into the latent space along the DDIM denoising trajectory, thereby decoupling the perturbation magnitude from pixel-level constraints and allowing perturbations to adaptively amplify where most effective. The extensible design of AEGIS allows the defense to be expanded from purely white-box use to also support black-box scenarios through a gradient-estimation strategy. Extensive experiments across GAN and diffusion-based deepfake generators show that AEGIS consistently delivers strong defense effectiveness while maintaining high perceptual quality. In white-box settings, it achieves robust manipulation disruption, whereas in black-box settings, it demonstrates strong cross-model transferability.

### [236] [Seclens: Role-specific Evaluation of LLM's for security vulnerablity detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01637)
*Subho Halder,Siddharth Saxena,Kashinath Kadaba Shrish,Thiyagarajan M*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: SecLens-R是一个多利益相关方评估框架，用于LLM漏洞检测，通过35个维度、7个测量类别和5种角色特定权重配置，为不同利益相关方提供定制化评估，而非单一指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM漏洞检测基准将模型性能压缩为单一指标，无法反映不同利益相关方（如CISO、工程主管、AI官员）的优先事项差异。需要更细粒度的评估框架来满足不同角色的需求。

Method: 提出SecLens-R框架，包含35个共享维度（分为7个测量类别），定义5种角色特定权重配置（CISO、首席AI官、安全研究员、工程主管、AI作为执行者）。每个配置选择12-16个维度，权重总和为80，产生0-100的决策分数。在406个任务（来自93个开源项目，覆盖10种编程语言和8种OWASP漏洞类别）上评估12个前沿模型，在代码提示和工具使用两种设置下进行。

Result: 不同利益相关方视角下的决策分数差异显著，同一模型在不同角色配置下分数差异可达31分。例如，Qwen3-Coder在工程主管配置下获得A级（76.3分），但在CISO配置下仅为D级（45.2分）。GPT-5.4也显示类似差异。这表明漏洞检测本质上是多目标问题，单一聚合指标会掩盖重要信息。

Conclusion: 漏洞检测评估需要考虑多利益相关方视角，SecLens-R框架能够提供比单一指标更丰富的见解，帮助不同角色根据其优先事项做出更明智的决策。

Abstract: Existing benchmarks for LLM-based vulnerability detection compress model performance into a single metric, which fails to reflect the distinct priorities of different stakeholders. For example, a CISO may emphasize high recall of critical vulnerabilities, an engineering leader may prioritize minimizing false positives, and an AI officer may balance capability against cost. To address this limitation, we introduce SecLens-R, a multi-stakeholder evaluation framework structured around 35 shared dimensions grouped into 7 measurement categories. The framework defines five role-specific weighting profiles: CISO, Chief AI Officer, Security Researcher, Head of Engineering, and AI-as-Actor. Each profile selects 12 to 16 dimensions with weights summing to 80, yielding a composite Decision Score between 0 and 100.
  We apply SecLens-R to evaluate 12 frontier models on a dataset of 406 tasks derived from 93 open-source projects, covering 10 programming languages and 8 OWASP-aligned vulnerability categories. Evaluations are conducted across two settings: Code-in-Prompt (CIP) and Tool-Use (TU). Results show substantial variation across stakeholder perspectives, with Decision Scores differing by as much as 31 points for the same model. For instance, Qwen3-Coder achieves an A (76.3) under the Head of Engineering profile but a D (45.2) under the CISO profile, while GPT-5.4 shows a similar disparity. These findings demonstrate that vulnerability detection is inherently a multi-objective problem and that stakeholder-aware evaluation provides insights that single aggregated metrics obscure.

</details>


### [237] [Combating Data Laundering in LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01904)
*Muxing Li,Zesheng Ye,Sharon Li,Feng Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文提出SDR方法，通过推断数据清洗变换并合成类似清洗数据的查询，增强对大型语言模型中未经授权数据使用的检测能力，即使数据所有者只有原始数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据清洗（data laundering）会改变专有数据的风格形式但保留关键信息，这使得基于性能差异的标准检测方法失效。当LLM仅使用清洗后的变体训练时，在原始数据上的表现不再更好，从而消除了检测信号。

Method: 提出合成数据还原（SDR）方法：1）从黑盒访问目标LLM推断未知的清洗变换；2）将变换抽象为高层次目标（如"抒情改写"）和具体细节（如"使用生动意象"）；3）首先识别最可能的合成目标来缩小搜索范围；4）迭代优化细节，使合成查询逐渐从目标LLM中引出更强的检测信号。

Result: 在MIMIR基准测试中，针对多种清洗实践和目标LLM家族（Pythia、Llama2、Falcon），SDR始终能增强数据滥用检测，为数据清洗提供了实用的应对措施。

Conclusion: SDR方法通过推断清洗变换并合成类似清洗数据的查询，有效应对数据清洗带来的检测挑战，为数据权利所有者提供了即使在只有原始数据的情况下也能检测未经授权数据使用的实用解决方案。

Abstract: Data rights owners can detect unauthorized data use in large language model (LLM) training by querying with proprietary samples. Often, superior performance (e.g., higher confidence or lower loss) on a sample relative to the untrained data implies it was part of the training corpus, as LLMs tend to perform better on data they have seen during training. However, this detection becomes fragile under data laundering, a practice of transforming the stylistic form of proprietary data, while preserving critical information to obfuscate data provenance. When an LLM is trained exclusively on such laundered variants, it no longer performs better on originals, erasing the signals that standard detections rely on. We counter this by inferring the unknown laundering transformation from black-box access to the target LLM and, via an auxiliary LLM, synthesizing queries that mimic the laundered data, even if rights owners have only the originals. As the search space of finding true laundering transformations is infinite, we abstract such a process into a high-level transformation goal (e.g., "lyrical rewriting") and concrete details (e.g., "with vivid imagery"), and introduce synthesis data reversion (SDR) that instantiates this abstraction. SDR first identifies the most probable goal for synthesis to narrow the search; it then iteratively refines details so that synthesized queries gradually elicit stronger detection signals from the target LLM. Evaluated on the MIMIR benchmark against diverse laundering practices and target LLM families (Pythia, Llama2, and Falcon), SDR consistently strengthens data misuse detection, providing a practical countermeasure to data laundering.

</details>


### [238] [From Component Manipulation to System Compromise: Understanding and Detecting Malicious MCP Servers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01905)
*Yiheng Huang,Zhijia Zhao,Bihuan Chen,Susheng Wu,Zhuotong Zhou,Yiheng Cao,Xin Hu,Xin Peng*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文提出组件中心视角来理解和检测恶意MCP服务器，构建首个组件中心PoC数据集，开发两阶段行为偏差检测器Connor，在恶意MCP服务器检测上达到94.6%的F1分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP（模型上下文协议）标准化了LLM连接外部工具和数据源的方式，虽然加快了集成速度，但也引入了新的攻击向量。现有MCP安全研究按可观察效果分类攻击，掩盖了攻击在不同MCP服务器组件中的行为，忽视了多组件攻击链。现有防御在面对多组件攻击或未知恶意行为时效果有限。

Method: 1. 构建首个组件中心的PoC数据集，包含114个恶意MCP服务器，攻击表现为对MCP组件及其组合的操纵。2. 提出并实现Connor，一个两阶段行为偏差检测器：第一阶段进行预执行分析，检测恶意shell命令并提取每个工具的功能意图；第二阶段进行逐步执行分析，追踪每个工具的行为轨迹并检测其与功能意图的偏差。

Result: 1. 在两个MCP主机和五个LLM上评估攻击有效性，发现：(1)组件位置影响攻击成功率；(2)多组件组合通常优于单组件攻击，通过分散恶意逻辑实现。2. Connor在构建的数据集上达到94.6%的F1分数，比现有最佳方法提升8.9%到59.6%。在实际检测中，Connor识别出两个恶意服务器。

Conclusion: 论文提出的组件中心视角能更好地理解和检测恶意MCP服务器，Connor检测器在识别恶意MCP服务器方面表现出色，特别是在处理多组件攻击和未知恶意行为方面具有优势。

Abstract: The model context protocol (MCP) standardizes how LLMs connect to external tools and data sources, enabling faster integration but introducing new attack vectors. Despite the growing adoption of MCP, existing MCP security studies classify attacks by their observable effects, obscuring how attacks behave across different MCP server components and overlooking multi-component attack chains. Meanwhile, existing defenses are less effective when facing multi-component attacks or previously unknown malicious behaviors.
  This work presents a component-centric perspective for understanding and detecting malicious MCP servers. First, we build the first component-centric PoC dataset of 114 malicious MCP servers where attacks are achieved as manipulation over MCP components and their compositions. We evaluate these attacks' effectiveness across two MCP hosts and five LLMs, and uncover that (1) component position shapes attack success rate; and (2) multi-component compositions often outperform single-component attacks by distributing malicious logic. Second, we propose and implement Connor, a two-stage behavioral deviation detector for malicious MCP servers. It first performs pre-execution analysis to detect malicious shell commands and extract each tool's function intent, and then conducts step-wise in-execution analysis to trace each tool's behavioral trajectories and detect deviations from its function intent. Evaluation on our curated dataset indicates that Connor achieves an F1-score of 94.6%, outperforming the state of the art by 8.9% to 59.6%. In real-world detection, Connor identifies two malicious servers.

</details>
